PART I: SECTION (I)  —  GENERAL 
 
Government Notifications 
1A - G 34232  - 30  (2021/04) 
THE SRI LANKA ARMED SERVICES LONG SERVICE MEDAL 
 
IT is hereby notified that His Excellency The President of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka and the 
Commander in Chief of the Armed Forces have been pleased to approve the award of the Sri Lanka Armed  Services 
Long Service Medal to the persons specified in the schedule here. 
   
    By His Excellency’s Command, 
 
 KAMAL GUNARATNE,  
 General (Rtd)  
 WWV RWP RSP USP ndc pscMPhil 
 Secretary, 
 Ministry of   Defence . 
Ministry of Defence, 
Colombo, 
21st April  2021.
